      '18': 'Retention',
      '19': 'Upsell',
      '20': 'Waner',
      '21': 'Live demo',
      '22': 'Premium',
      '23': 'MQL',
    };
    var products = {
      '1': 'Cisco Spark',
      '2': 'Collaboration Meeting Rooms (CMR)',
      '3': 'Collaboration Solutions',
      '4': 'WebEx Event Center',
      '5': 'WebEx Meeting Center',
      '6': 'WebEx Meetings',
      '7': 'WebEx Training Center',
      '8': 'WebEx Support Center',
      '9': 'Project Storm',
      '10': 'MC+Spark',
      '11': 'Spark Board',
    };

    var getCountry = function (value) {
      var country = invalid;

      // Format values properly.
      if (/^[a-z]{2}$/i.test(value)) {
        country = value.toUpperCase();
      } else if (/^Global$/i.test(value)) {
        country = 'Global';
      }

      return country;
    };

    var lookup = function (key, values) {
      var cleanedKey = cleanKey(key);
      var value = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(values, cleanedKey) ? values[cleanedKey] : invalid;

      return value;
    };

    var trimLeadingZeroes = function (s) {
      return s.replace(/^0+/, '');
    };

    var cleanKey = function (s) {
      // A key must have 1-4 digits. We will trim any leading zeroes for subsequent lookup.
      var validKey = /^\d{1,4}$/;
      var cleaned = s;

      if (validKey.test(cleaned)) {
        cleaned = trimLeadingZeroes(cleaned);
      } else {
        cleaned = invalid;
      }

      return cleaned;
    };

    var validateDgid = function (dgid) {
      // DGID key should have 8 positions delimited by "-".
      var isValid = false;

      if (typeof dgid === 'string') {
        isValid = dgid.split('-').length === 8;
      }

      return isValid;
    };

    var decodeDgid = function (dgid) {
      var isValidDgid = validateDgid(dgid);
      var keys;
      var decoded = {};
      var dgFunction = invalid;
      var dgChannel = invalid;
      var dgPlacement = invalid;
      var dgCountry = invalid;
      var dgChannelTactic = invalid;
      var dgPersona = invalid;
      var dgGoal = invalid;
      var dgProduct = invalid;

      if (isValidDgid) {
        try {
          keys = dgid.split('-');
          dgFunction = lookup(keys[0], functions);
          dgChannel = lookup(keys[1], channels);
          dgPlacement = lookup(keys[2], placements);
          dgCountry = getCountry(keys[3]);
          dgChannelTactic = lookup(keys[4], channelTactics);
          dgPersona = lookup(keys[5], personas);
          dgGoal = lookup(keys[6], goals);
          dgProduct = lookup(keys[7], products);
        } catch (e) {
          // Do nothing.
        }
      }

      decoded = {
        dg_function: dgFunction,
        dg_channel: dgChannel,
        dg_placement: dgPlacement,
        dg_country: dgCountry,
        dg_channel_tactic: dgChannelTactic,
        dg_persona: dgPersona,
        dg_goal: dgGoal,
        dg_product: dgProduct,
      };

      return decoded;
    };

    var getDGID = function () {
      // In order of preference, check DG, then DGID parameters.
      var dgid = {};
      dgid.key = utilURL.parameter('DG');
      if (dgid.key === '') {
        dgid.key = utilURL.parameter('DGID');
      }
      dgid.decoded = decodeDgid(dgid.key);

      return dgid;
    };

    var init = (function () {
      data = getDGID();
    })();

    return {
      data: data,
    };
  })();
  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
  var utilUTM = (function () {
    var urlParameters;
    var hasUrlParameters;

    var getUrlParameters = function () {
      // UTM Source: PaidSearch, PaidSocial, Programmatic, OrganicSocial etc.
      // UTM Channel: GoogleAds / FacebookAds / TwitterAds etc
      // UTM Campaign: Campaign name
      // UTM Content: Ad Set / Ad Group
      // UTM Medium: Ad name
      parameters = {
        campaign: utilURL.parameter('utm_campaign'),
        channel: utilURL.parameter('utm_channel'),
        content: utilURL.parameter('utm_content'),
        medium: utilURL.parameter('utm_medium'),
        source: utilURL.parameter('utm_source'),
        term: utilURL.parameter('utm_term'),
      };

      return parameters;
    };

    var init = (function () {
      var p;
      urlParameters = getUrlParameters();

      hasUrlParameters = false;
      for (p in urlParameters) {
        if (urlParameters[p].length > 0) {
          hasUrlParameters = true;
          break;
        }
      }
    })();

    return {
      parameters: urlParameters,
      hasParameters: hasUrlParameters,
    };
  })();
  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // post-meeting landing page
  var pmlp = (function () {
    var data = {};

    var getUserType = function () {
      var url = utilURL.urlCleaned;
      var userType = '';
      if (/\/post-meeting\/host\//.test(url)) {
        userType = 'host';
      } else if (/\/post-meeting\/attendee\//.test(url)) {
        userType = 'attendee';
      } else if (/\/post-meeting\/index\.html/.test(url)) {
        userType = utilURL.parameter('userType').toLowerCase() || '';
      }

      return userType;
    };

    var getData = function () {
      var data = {
        billingMode: utilURL.parameter('billingMode'),
        userType: getUserType(),
      };

      return data;
    };

    var isPmlp;

    var init = (function () {
      data = getData();

      isPmlp = data.userType !== '';
    })();

    return {
      data: data,
      isPmlp: isPmlp,
    };
  })();
  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
  var deviceInfo = (function () {
    var data = {};

    var getData = function () {
      var getBucket = function (x) {
        var bucketSize = 100;

        var lowerBound = Math.floor(x / bucketSize);
        var upperBound = (lowerBound + 1) * bucketSize - 1;

        var value = lowerBound * bucketSize + ' to ' + upperBound;

        return value;
      };

      var monitor = {
        width: window.screen.width,
        height: window.screen.height,
      };
      monitor.width_bucketed = getBucket(monitor.width);
      monitor.height_bucketed = getBucket(monitor.height);

      var viewport = {
        width: window.innerWidth,
        height: window.innerHeight,
      };
      viewport.width_bucketed = getBucket(viewport.width);
      viewport.height_bucketed = getBucket(viewport.height);

      var data = {
        screen: monitor,
        viewport: viewport,
      };

      return data;
    };

    var init = (function () {
      data = getData();
    })();

    return {
      data: data,
    };
  })();
  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

  var getReferrerURL = function () {
    var url = document.referrer || '';

    url = utilURL.clean(url);

    return url;
  };

  var getReferrerDomain = function () {
    var domain;
    var url = document.referrer;

    var matches = url.match(/:\/\/(.[^/]+)/);

    if (matches !== null && matches[1] !== null) {
      domain = matches[1];
    } else {
      domain = '';
    }

    return domain;
  };

  var getReferrerChannel = function () {
    var domain = getReferrerDomain();
    var patternDirect = /^$/;
    var patternInternal = /(blog|help)\.webex\.com/i;
    // Use none to bucket exclusions with all lower environment, webex.co.*, and non- blog. and help. webex.com traffic.
    var patternNone = /(wbxapp-(auth|pub)-|origin-webex-[a-z]+.cisco\.com|\.webex\.co\.|(?!blog|help)\.webex\.com)/i;
    var patternSearch = /\.(aol|ask|askjeeves|baidu|bing|chacha|duckduckgo|excite|google|lycos|msxml|searchencrypt|yahoo|yandex)\./i;
    var patternSocial = /\.(facebook|linkedin)\.com/i;
    var channels = {
      direct: 'direct',
      internal: 'internal',
      none: 'none',
      other: 'other',
      search: 'search engine',
      social: 'social',
    };
    var channel = channels.other;

    if (patternDirect.test(domain)) {
      channel = channels.direct;
    } else if (patternInternal.test(domain)) {
      channel = channels.internal;
    } else if (patternNone.test(domain)) {
      channel = channels.none;
    } else if (patternSearch.test(domain)) {
      channel = channels.search;
    } else if (patternSocial.test(domain)) {
      channel = channels.social;
    }

    if (/^(search engine|social)$/i.test(channel)) {
      channel = isPaidTraffic() ? channel + ' - paid' : channel + ' - organic';
    }

    return channel;
  };

  var isPaidTraffic = function () {
    // Check if any of the following values exist.
    var isPaid = utilDGID.data.key !== '' || utilUTM.hasParameters;

    return isPaid;
  };

  var getTargeterValue = function (property) {
    var value;
    try {
      value = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('targeter')).for_analysis[property];
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var getPageName = function () {
    var name;

    var isFile = function (url) {
      var value = /^file:\/\//i.test(url);
      return value;
    };

    var isPageNotFound = function () {
      value = false;
      var translationPageNotFound = [
        'Page not Found', // en
        'Seite nicht gefunden', // de
        'Pgina no encontrada', // es
        'Page non trouve', // fr
        ' - Cisco Webex', // ja
        'Pgina no encontrada', // pt
        '', // zh_CN
        '', // zh_HK
        'Page not Found',
        '   ', // ko
        'No se encontr la pgina.', // es_MX
      ];
      var metaTitle;

      try {
        metaTitle = document.querySelector('meta[name=title]').content.toLowerCase();
      } catch (e) {
        metaTitle = '';
      }

      if (metaTitle !== '') {
        for (var i = 0; i < translationPageNotFound.length; i++) {
          value = translationPageNotFound[i].toLowerCase().indexOf(metaTitle) > -1;
          if (value) break;
        }
      }

      return value;
    };

    var url = document.URL;

    name = isPageNotFound()
      ? 'page-not-found'
      : isFile(url)
      ? 'file'
      : /www\.webex\.com\/join\//i.test(url)
      ? 'join'
      : /www\.webex\.com\/meet\//i.test(url)
      ? 'meet'
      : _satellite.getVar('p_n').replace(':', '');

    return name;
  };

  var getPageCategory = function () {
    return '';
  };

  var gatherData = function () {
    var dgid = utilDGID.data;
    var utm = utilUTM.parameters;
    var isPaid = isPaidTraffic();
    var device = deviceInfo.data;
    var cleanedURL = utilURL.urlCleaned;
    var data = {
      pageName: getPageName(),
      pageCategory: getPageCategory(),
      destinationURL: cleanedURL,
      referringURL: getReferrerURL(),
      referringDomain: getReferrerDomain(),
      referringChannel: getReferrerChannel(),
      param_utm: utm,
      param_DGID: dgid,
      param_psearchID: utilURL.parameter('psearchID'),
      param_segment: utilURL.parameter('segment'),
      param_team: utilURL.parameter('team'),
      param_trackID: utilURL.parameter('TrackID'),
      isPaidTraffic: isPaid,
      device: device,
    };

    var mainUrl = cleanedURL
      .replace(/[\?|#].+/, '')
      .replace(/[?]/g, '')
      .replace(/^http(s?):\/\//i, '');
    var fullUrl = cleanedURL.replace(/^http(s?):\/\//i, '');
    var userLang = document.querySelector("html").lang || '';
    var userLocale;
    if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.co.in') > 0) userLocale = 'in';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.com.cn') > 0) userLocale = 'cn';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.com.br') > 0) userLocale = 'br';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.com.mx/') > 0) userLocale = 'mx';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.co.kr/') > 0) userLocale = 'kr';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.es/') > 0) userLocale = 'es';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.co.it/') > 0) userLocale = 'it';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.com/it/') > 0) userLocale = 'it';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.com/es/') > 0) userLocale = 'es';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.com/ko/') > 0) userLocale = 'ko';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.com/hk/') > 0) userLocale = 'it';
    else if (cleanedURL.indexOf('/www.webex.com/br/') > 0) userLocale = 'br';
    else userLocale = _satellite.cookie.get('user_locale') || '';

    userLang = userLang.toLowerCase();
    userLocale = userLocale.toLowerCase();

    // Add to the data object.
    data.pageViewedEventProperties = {
      page_name: data.pageName,
      page_category: data.pageCategory,
      custom_referrer_url: data.referringURL,
      main_page_url: mainUrl,
      page_url: fullUrl,
      domain: location.host,
      locale: userLocale,
      lang: userLang,
      dg_param: data.param_DGID.key,
      param_segment: data.param_segment,
      param_team: data.param_team,
      trackID: data.param_trackID,
      psearchID: data.param_psearchID,
    };

    data.targeter = {
      domain: getTargeterValue('domain'),
      company_name: getTargeterValue('company_name'),
      company_size: getTargeterValue('company_size'),
      industry_category: getTargeterValue('industry_category'),
      industry_sub_category: getTargeterValue('industry_sub_category'),
      segment: getTargeterValue('segment'),
    };

    if (pmlp.isPmlp) {
      data.pmlp = pmlp.data;
      data.pageViewedEventProperties.pmlp_user_type = data.pmlp.userType;
      data.pageViewedEventProperties.pmlp_billing_mode = data.pmlp.billingMode;
    }

    return data;
  };

  var init = (function () {
    gathered = gatherData();
  })();

  return {
    gathered: gathered,
    utilURL: utilURL,
  };
})();

var utilDataLayer = (function (data) {
  var digitalData = {};

  var getProperty = function (p) {
    var value;

    try {
      value = data[p] || '';
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var hasUtm = function (utm) {
    var hasUtm = utm.campaign + utm.channel + utm.content + utm.medium + utm.source !== '';

    return hasUtm;
  };

  var setDigitalData = function () {
    var pageName = getProperty('pageName');
    var pageCategory = getProperty('pageCategory');
    var destinationURL = getProperty('destinationURL');
    var referringURL = getProperty('referringURL');
    var referringDomain = getProperty('referringDomain');
    var referringChannel = getProperty('referringChannel');
    var param_demandGeneration = getProperty('param_DGID');
    var param_psearchID = getProperty('param_psearchID');
    var param_segment = getProperty('param_segment');
    var param_team = getProperty('param_team');
    var param_TrackID = getProperty('param_trackID');
    var param_utm = getProperty('param_utm');
    var targeter = getProperty('targeter');
    var device = getProperty('device');

    digitalData = {
      page: {
        pageInfo: {
          pageName: pageName,
          pageCategory: pageCategory,
          destinationURL: destinationURL,
          referringURL: referringURL,
          referringDomain: referringDomain,
          referringChannel: referringChannel,
        },
      },
      user: [
        {
          profile: [
            {
              device: device,
            },
          ],
          segment: {},
        },
      ],
    };
    var userProperties = digitalData.user[0].segment;

    // Only add user properties that exist.
    if (param_demandGeneration.key !== '') userProperties.demandGeneration = param_demandGeneration;
    if (hasUtm(param_utm)) userProperties.param_utm = param_utm;
    if (param_segment !== '') userProperties.param_segment = param_segment;
    if (param_team !== '') userProperties.param_team = param_team;
    if (param_TrackID !== '') userProperties.param_TrackID = param_TrackID;
    if (param_psearchID !== '') userProperties.param_psearchID = param_psearchID;
    if (targeter !== '') userProperties.targeter = targeter;
  };

  var init = (function () {
    setDigitalData();
  })();

  return {
    digitalData: digitalData,
  };
})(webex.util.data.gathered);

(function (data) {
  var getDGKey = function () {
    var value;

    try {
      value = data.param_DGID.key || '';
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var getDeviceProperty = function (p, sub_p) {
    var value;

    try {
      value = data.device[p][sub_p] || '';
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var getDGProperty = function (p) {
    var value;

    try {
      value = data.param_DGID.decoded[p] || '';
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var getPmlpProperty = function (p) {
    var value;

    try {
      value = data.pmlp[p] || '';
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var getTargeterProperty = function (p) {
    var value;

    try {
      value = data.targeter[p] || '';
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var getUtmProperty = function (p) {
    var value;

    try {
      value = data.param_utm[p] || '';
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var getProperty = function (p) {
    var value;

    try {
      value = data[p] || '';
    } catch (e) {
      value = '';
    }

    return value;
  };

  var setTargeterProperty = function (property, userProperties) {
    // If 'property' exists in targeter, add it to 'userProperties'.
    var value = getTargeterProperty(property);

    if (value !== '') userProperties['targeter.' + property] = value;

    return userProperties;
  };

  var getPageSubdomain = function (host) {
    var splits = host.split('.');
    var subdomain = splits[0];
    var domain;
    try {
      domain = splits[1];
    } catch (e) {
      domain = '';
    }
    
    if (/^webexone$/.test(domain)) {
      subdomain = 'www.webexone';
    } else {
      subdomain = /webex/.test(subdomain) ? '' : subdomain;
    }

    return subdomain;
  }

  var getPageCategory = function (url) {
    var pageCategory = '';
    var path;
    var steps;
    var localizedPaths = /^\/(de|es|fr|it|ja|ko|pt|zh-tw)\//i;
    var isLocalized;
    var topDirectory;

    if (getProperty('pageName') === "page-not-found") {
      pageCategory = getProperty('pageName');
    } else if (getProperty('pageCategory') !== '') {
      pageCategory = getProperty('pageCategory')
    } else {
      // Find top-level directory.
      path = url.split(".com")[1];
      path = path.split('#')[0]; // discard hash
      path = path.split('?')[0]; // discard query string
      isLocalized = localizedPaths.test(path);
      steps = path.split('/');
      if (isLocalized) {
        topDirectory = steps.length > 3 ? steps[2] : '';
      } else {
        topDirectory = steps.length > 2 ? steps[1] : '';
      }
      pageCategory = decodeURIComponent(topDirectory);
    }

    return pageCategory
  }

  var getEventName = function (domain, url) {
    var prefix = "pageviewed"
    var pageSubdomain = getPageSubdomain(domain);
    var pageCategory = getPageCategory(url);

    var eventName = prefix + ":" + pageSubdomain + ":" + pageCategory;

    return eventName;
  }

  var getEventNameCustom = function (url) {
    var eventName = '';
    var urlsWithOtherPageViewEvents = /www\.webex\.com\/pricing\/buy\//i;
    if (!urlsWithOtherPageViewEvents.test(url)) {
      eventName = /free_to_paid/i.test(url)
        ? 'MCOnline_CO_pricing page upgrade viewed'
        : '';
    }

    return(eventName);
  }

  var send = function () {
    var userProperties = {};
    var eventName;
    var pageViewEventProperties = getProperty('pageViewedEventProperties');
    var param_segment = getProperty('param_segment');
    var param_team = getProperty('param_team');
    var param_TrackID = getProperty('param_trackID');
    var param_psearchID = getProperty('param_psearchID');
    var referringURL = getProperty('referringURL');
    var referringDomain = getProperty('referringDomain');
    var referringChannel = getProperty('referringChannel');
    var utmChannel = getUtmProperty('channel');
    var pmlpBillingMode = getPmlpProperty('billingMode');
    var pmlpUserType = getPmlpProperty('userType');
    var sendParamPsearchId = param_psearchID !== '';
    var sendParamSegment = param_segment !== '';
    var sendParamTeam = param_team !== '';
    var sendReferringChannel = referringChannel !== '' && referringChannel !== 'none';
    var sendUtmChannel = utmChannel !== '';
    var identifyAmp;

    // Make sure Amplitude is loaded. Exclude lightboxes.
    if (typeof amplitude !== 'undefined' && document.URL.indexOf('/lbx/') < 0) {
      identifyAmp = new amplitude.Identify();

      userProperties.screen_height = getDeviceProperty('screen', 'height');
      userProperties.screen_width = getDeviceProperty('screen', 'width');
      userProperties.screen_height_bucketed = getDeviceProperty('screen', 'height_bucketed');
      userProperties.screen_width_bucketed = getDeviceProperty('screen', 'width_bucketed');
      userProperties.viewport_height = getDeviceProperty('viewport', 'height');
      userProperties.viewport_width = getDeviceProperty('viewport', 'width');
      userProperties.viewport_height_bucketed = getDeviceProperty('viewport', 'height_bucketed');
      userProperties.viewport_width_bucketed = getDeviceProperty('viewport', 'width_bucketed');

      // If not a PMLP, clear PMLP user properties.
      if (pmlpBillingMode === '') {
        identifyAmp.unset('pmlp_billing_mode');
      } else {
        userProperties.pmlp_billing_mode = pmlpBillingMode;
      }
      if (pmlpUserType === '') {
        identifyAmp.unset('pmlp_user_type');
      } else {
        userProperties.pmlp_user_type = pmlpUserType;
      }
      // Only add user properties that exist.
      if (getProperty('isPaidTraffic')) {
        userProperties.DGID = getDGKey();
        userProperties.dg_function = getDGProperty('dg_function');
        userProperties.dg_channel = getDGProperty('dg_channel');
        userProperties.dg_placement = getDGProperty('dg_placement');
        userProperties.dg_country = getDGProperty('dg_country');
        userProperties.dg_channel_tactic = getDGProperty('dg_channel_tactic');
        userProperties.dg_persona = getDGProperty('dg_persona');
        userProperties.dg_goal = getDGProperty('dg_goal');
        userProperties.dg_product = getDGProperty('dg_product');
      }
      if (param_TrackID !== '') userProperties.TrackID = param_TrackID;
      // Amplitude's referring URL can include PII. Ours does not. Use ours.
      if (referringURL !== '') userProperties.referrer = referringURL;
      // Use Amplitude's referring domain.
      // if (referringDomain !== '') userProperties.referring_domain = referringDomain;

      if (sendParamPsearchId || sendParamSegment || sendParamTeam || sendReferringChannel || sendUtmChannel) {
        // Set the initial and last-touch values for each of these user properties.
        if (sendParamPsearchId) {
          identifyAmp.setOnce('initial_psearchID', param_psearchID);
          userProperties.psearchID = param_psearchID;
        }
        if (sendParamSegment) {
          identifyAmp.setOnce('initial_url_param_segment', param_segment);
          userProperties.url_param_segment = param_segment;
        }
        if (sendParamTeam) {
          identifyAmp.setOnce('initial_url_param_team', param_team);
          userProperties.url_param_team = param_team;
        }
        if (sendReferringChannel) {
          identifyAmp.setOnce('initial_referring_channel', referringChannel);
          userProperties.referring_channel = referringChannel;
        }
        if (sendUtmChannel) {
          identifyAmp.setOnce('initial_utm_channel', utmChannel);
          userProperties.utm_channel = utmChannel;
        }
        // Make a single, combined .identify() call.
        amplitude.getInstance().identify(identifyAmp);

        userProperties = setTargeterProperty('domain', userProperties);
        userProperties = setTargeterProperty('company_name', userProperties);
        userProperties = setTargeterProperty('company_size', userProperties);
        userProperties = setTargeterProperty('industry_category', userProperties);
        userProperties = setTargeterProperty('industry_sub_category', userProperties);
        userProperties = setTargeterProperty('segment', userProperties);
      }

      // Send the user properties to Amplitude.
      amplitude.getInstance().setUserProperties(userProperties);

      eventName = getEventName(document.domain, document.URL);
      amplitude.getInstance().logEvent(eventName, pageViewEventProperties);
      // Send custom event name, if any.
      eventName = getEventNameCustom(document.URL);
      if (eventName !== '') {
        amplitude.getInstance().logEvent(eventName, pageViewEventProperties);
      }
    }
  };

  var init = (function () {
    send();
  })();
})(webex.util.data.gathered);

var webex = webex || {};
webex.util = webex.util || {};
webex.util.click = (function() {
  var clickables;
  var clickEventName = 'wx_clicked';
  var utilURL = webex.util.data.utilURL;
  var pageView = webex.util.data.gathered.pageViewedEventProperties;

  var onClick = function(event, eventProperties) {
    try {
      amplitude.getInstance().logEvent(clickEventName, eventProperties);
    } catch (e) {
      // Do nothing.
    }
    return false;
  };

  var configure = function(el) {
    var clickId = el.getAttribute('data-click-id');
    var destination = (typeof el.href !== 'undefined') ? utilURL.clean(el.href) : '';
    var eventProperties = {
      page_url: pageView.page_url,
      page_name: pageView.page_name,
      click_ID: clickId,
      destination: destination,
    };

    el.addEventListener(
      'click',
      function(el) {
        onClick(el, eventProperties);
      },
      false
    );
  };

  var getClickables = function() {
    var clickables = document.querySelectorAll('[data-click-id]');

    return clickables;
  };

  var init = (function() {
    clickables = getClickables();
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(clickables, configure);
  })();

  return {
    configure: configure,
  };
})();

webex.chat =
  webex.chat ||
  (function () {
    var config = {
      new: {
        urlDestination: 'https://spyder.cisco.com/app/v2/chat?id=MTAwMDA1&source=webex.com',
        window: {
          name: '_blank',
          options: 'location=no,left=0,right=0,width=425,height=800',
        },
      },
      legacy: {
        urlScript: '/content/dam/webex/eopi/lib/LiveAgent/c2c-standalone-v8-2-5-webex-b.js',
      },
    };

    var loadScript = function (url) {
      var script = document.createElement('script');

      script.type = 'text/javascript';
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
    };

    var getQueryParams = function (qs) {
      qs = qs.split('+').join(' ');

      var params = {},
        tokens,
        re = /[?&]?([^=]+)=([^&]*)/g;

      while ((tokens = re.exec(qs))) {
        params[decodeURIComponent(tokens[1])] = decodeURIComponent(tokens[2]);
      }

      return params;
    };

    var getCookie = function (cname) {
      var name = cname + '=';
      var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
      var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
      for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
          c = c.substring(1);
        }
        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
          return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
        }
      }
      return '';
    };

    var getCountryCode = function (locale) {
      var splits = locale.split('_');
      var countryCode = splits.length > 1 ? splits[1] : '';
      return countryCode.toUpperCase();
    };

    var getLanguage = function (locale) {
      var splits = locale.split('_');
      var language = splits.length > 1 ? splits[0] : '';
      return language.toLowerCase();
    };

    var getLocale = function () {
      var lang;
      var country;
      var qs;
      var locale;
      var domain = document.domain.toLowerCase();

      switch (domain) {
        case 'www.webex.co.kr':
          locale = 'ko_KR';
          break;
        case 'www.webex.co.in':
          locale = 'en_IN';
          break;
        case 'www.webex.com.br':
          locale = 'pt_BR';
          break;
        case 'www.webex.com.cn':
          locale = 'zh_CN';
          break;
        case 'www.webex.com.hk':
          locale = 'zh_HK';
          break;
        case 'www.webex.com.mx':
          locale = 'es_MX';
          break;
        default:
          // www.webex.com
          lang = getCookie('user_lang') || 'en';
          country = getCookie('user_locale') || 'US';
          locale = lang + '_' + country;
      }

      // Locale override.
      qs = getQueryParams(document.location.search);
      locale = qs.test_locale || locale;

      return locale;
    };

    var doChatIMI = function (locale) {
      var elButton = document.querySelector('.c2c-component .c2c-active .c2c-button');

      // Remove chat button.
      if (elButton !== null) {
        elButton.remove();
      }
    };

    var doChatWCA = function (locale) {
      var elActive = document.querySelector('.c2c-component .c2c-active');
      var elButton = document.querySelector('.c2c-component .c2c-active .c2c-button');
      var chatDelay = 0;

      var countryCode = getCountryCode(locale);
      // The chat bot uses KO instead of KR for South Korea.
      if (countryCode === 'KR') countryCode = 'KO';

      if (elButton !== null) {
        // Create button click handler.
        elButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
          var url = config.new.urlDestination + '&CountryInput=' + countryCode;
          window.open(url, config.new.window.name, config.new.window.options);
        });

        // Display chat button.
        // Tealium will hide the chat. Introduce a delay to show the chat after Tealium would have hidden it.
        setTimeout(function () {
          try {
            elActive.style.display = 'block';
          } catch (e) {
            // Do nothing.
          }
        }, chatDelay);
      }
    };

    var doChatLegacy = function () {
      // load script file.
      loadScript(config.legacy.urlScript);
    };

    var removeElement = function (el) {
      if (el !== null) {
        el.parentNode.removeChild(el);
      }
    };

    var replaceMetaTag = function (name, content) {
      var elHead = document.querySelector('head');
      var elMetaOld = elHead.querySelector('meta[name=' + name + ']');
      var elMetaNew = document.createElement('meta');

      elMetaNew.setAttribute('name', name);
      elMetaNew.setAttribute('content', content);

      removeElement(elMetaOld);
      elHead.appendChild(elMetaNew);
    };

    var localizeMetaTags = function (locale) {
      // If LiveAgent cannot determine the user's locale, it reads meta tags.
      // The locale meta tag uses the same value as the country meta tag.
      var language = getLanguage(locale);
      var countryCode = getCountryCode(locale);

      replaceMetaTag('locale', countryCode);
      replaceMetaTag('language', language);
      replaceMetaTag('country', countryCode);
    };

    var supportsWCA = function (locale) {
      var reLocalesSupported = /^(en_(?!gb|it|uk)[a-z]{2}|ja_JP|ko_KR|zh-tw_HK)$/i;
      // en_GB, en_IT, en_UK have dedicated legacy chat queues.
      // Send all other en_ locales to chat bot.
      var isSupported = reLocalesSupported.test(locale);

      return isSupported;
    };

    var supportsIMI = function (locale) {
      var reLocalesSupported = /^en_(au|ca|gb|in|uk|us)$/i;

      var isSupported = reLocalesSupported.test(locale);

      return isSupported;
    };

    var sendMetricChat = function (assignedChat) {
      try {
        amplitude.getInstance().logEvent('chat_assigned', {version: assignedChat});
      } catch (e) {
        console.log('chat:' + assignedChat + ':' + e.message);
      }
    };

    var init = (function () {
      var locale = getLocale();
      localizeMetaTags(locale);

      if (supportsIMI(locale)) {
        doChatIMI(locale);
        sendMetricChat('IMI');
      } else if (supportsWCA(locale)) {
        doChatWCA(locale);
        sendMetricChat('WCA');
      } else {
        doChatLegacy();
        sendMetricChat('Legacy');
      }
    })();
  })();
